(15) Qianjiang: One breach occurred in the Min Dike of the Zhilu River, and the Meijiazui Dike collapsed completely. The ninth district was severely affected. (16) Mianyang: The dikes of the three major river basins, Dongkai River, Shuntong River, and Chailin River, collapsed continuously. Most of Xiantao Town was submerged, and tens of thousands of people were in need of special relief. (17) Hanchuan: The entire Ximakou Gaohu Dike collapsed, affecting Xiangbenyuan, Hejiayuan, and Xujiayuan. Many shops on Ximakou Street were destroyed, and more than 20 people were drowned. The Yongshu, Huanggong, Renhe, Fafu, Xiangxing, Tiancheng, Yongfeng, Taihe, and Baishi Juyuan collapsed one after another. The houses and crops inside the dikes were completely submerged, and many people and animals were killed or injured. More than 700 miles were turned into a swamp. (18) Hanyang: The north was slightly affected by the flood in Hanchuan, and the south suffered from drought. (19) Shishou: It has not rained for more than a month, and the harvest is hopeless. Rice prices have soared, and people's food is worrisome. (20) Jianli: The dike collapsed, and half of the area was flooded. (21) Yunmeng: Six breaches occurred in the Tanhu Dike, and the entire county was flooded. Many people and animals were drowned. (22) Wuchang: The land is scorched, and the crops are withered. The harvest is hopeless, and disaster victims are asking to leave the area to beg for food. (23) Puqi: Severe drought has caused most crops to be scorched to death, and the autumn harvest is hopeless. (24) Chongyang: The crops are withered, the fields are cracked, and there is a lack of food. (25) Tongcheng: Two mountain floods flooded a very wide area. (26) Xianning: It has not rained for a long time, and the ditches are dry. The crops are withered, and the disaster is severe. (27) Yangxin: The entire territory is affected by drought, and rice, grain, and beans are dead. (28) Daye: It has not rained for a long time, and the drought is widespread. (29) Echeng: The drought is severe, the water sources are exhausted, the fields are cracked, and the crops are withered. (30) Qichun: It has not rained for a long time, and all districts are affected by drought. (31) Huangmei: The crops are withered, the water supply is cut off, and locusts have recently been discovered, which will spread throughout the territory. (32) Guangji: It was repeatedly flooded in the spring, and suffered severe drought in the summer. Recently, there has been a dragon disaster, and the people are panicked. All taxes have been suspended. (33) Yingshan: The drought has become a disaster, and refugees are waiting for relief. (34) Lishan: Mountain floods broke out, and the fields were flooded. (35) Huanggang: The drought has spread throughout the county, and people are panicking. (36) Macheng: The drought is very severe, and the fields in districts 1, 5, 6, and 7 are half withered. (37) Huang'an: The fields are dry, the crops are withered, and people's food is worrisome. (38) Luotian: Fertile land is cracked, and mountain forests are withered. The disaster has spread throughout the territory. (39) Xishui: It has not rained for two months, and the ponds are dry. High ground has become dust, and low fields have turned into withered grass. (40) Huangpi: The drought demon is rampant, and the entire territory is a disaster. The above is a rough count, reaching 40 counties. Among them, Huang'an, Lishan, Yangxin, Qianjiang, Lichuan, and Hefeng counties have long suffered from bandit disasters, and their vitality has not yet recovered. A famine in a bad year is also expected. (July 23)

Chairman Chiang Explains the Meaning of Wuyuan's Reassignment 101

Political, Military, and Highway Conveniences are All Greatly Enhanced

Requesting Exemption from Reassignment Shows Narrow-Mindedness and a Lack of Understanding

Order to the Wuyuan County Government to Conduct Extensive Propaganda and Guidance

Nanchang Dispatch: Chairman Chiang's headquarters, in order to facilitate military, political, and highway matters in Anhui's Wuyuan County, which protrudes into Jiangxi Province, has decided to place it under the jurisdiction of Jiangxi, and has filed a record with the Executive Yuan, ordering the governments of Jiangxi and Anhui provinces to send personnel to hand over the area. It is now learned that the various Wuyuan fellow-countrymen's associations abroad have sent letters to the headquarters requesting exemption from reassignment. After receiving the letters, the headquarters, after examining the reasons for the request, found them to be based on narrow-minded views and a lack of deep understanding of the purpose of the reassignment. It has specifically ordered the Wuyuan County government to explain the various points in the order and to provide detailed guidance. The original order is as follows:

"It has been found that the case of the reassignment of the county to Jiangxi Province has already been ordered by this headquarters to the governments of Jiangxi and Anhui provinces to hand over the area and establish boundary markers separately, and a letter has been sent to the Executive Yuan to order the responsible departments to record the case in the files. Subsequently, the Ziyang Academy of the county, as well as the Wuyuan fellow-countrymen's associations in Beijing, Shanghai, Wuxi, and Xiuning, have successively sent letters and telegrams requesting exemption from reassignment. After examining the reasons given, they are based on narrow-minded views and a lack of deep understanding of the purpose of the reassignment. The following is a specific explanation:

Reasons for the Necessary Reassignment 102

The most important reasons why Wuyuan must be reassigned are approximately three: (A) Politically, it has been found that Wuyuan was established as a county during the reign of Emperor Xuanzong of the Tang Dynasty and belonged to She Prefecture of Jiangnan Dao. During the Song Dynasty, it was proposed to reassign it to Jiangxi Province because the rivers south of the county all flowed into Jiangxi, using Maoling and Xinling as boundaries. Now, observing its terrain, most of it protrudes into Jiangxi Province and is surrounded by the three counties of Fuliang, Leping, and Dexing. It feels very isolated from Anhui Province, and all administrative facilities are inconvenient. If it is not reassigned, it will be restricted by the current situation and unable to expand its political power. (B) Militarily, at a time when the work of suppressing bandits is particularly tense, eliminating remnant bandits is an urgent task. Wuyuan and the three counties of Fuliang, Leping, and Dexing are geographically intertwined. Due to their belonging to two different provinces, all necessary measures to eliminate remnant bandits, such as the defense of local militias and encirclement plans, are greatly separated, giving the Red bandits opportunities to flee and prolong their survival. Once reassigned, authority will belong to one province, responsibility will be focused, and command will be more convenient. The extermination of the remaining bandits can be expected in the near future. (C) In terms of highways, the Wubai and Wude roads, one from Wuyuan through Jiudu of Dexing to Baishaguan, and the other from Wuyuan to Tuntan of Dexing, are closely related to bandit suppression, military affairs, and local transportation. If Wuyuan is not assigned to Jiangxi, the two roads will belong to two provinces, and transportation management will be difficult to coordinate. At this time when the bandit crisis has not yet been resolved, we must not allow any slackness that could delay the opportunity. All three of these points are extremely clear. The order from this headquarters to reassign the county is truly in accordance with the principles of adapting to local conditions and adapting to the situation, and is carefully considered and truly in line with the requirements.

Refuting Opposing Reasons 103

The reasons given by the various Wuyuan groups for opposing the reassignment are far-fetched in both theory and fact and have been refuted separately. The main points are as follows: (A) Different Customs: The main point is that although Wuyuan is adjacent to Leping and Dexing in Jiangxi, its customs are very different. If reassignment is carried out, there will be many problems with administrative facilities. It is found that China's transportation is not yet developed, so there is inevitably a phenomenon of "no communication within a hundred miles." Wuyuan protrudes into the three counties of Delefu in Jiangxi. The customs of the border areas should not be very different. Anhui Province has more than 60 counties, and the language and customs of Wuyuan, except for the two or three counties of Xiu and She in its vicinity, are not the same as those of other counties. Even in the old Huizhou Prefecture, which belongs to six counties, I am afraid there will be conflicts. This cannot be a reason. (B) Economic Reality: Regarding political groups, organizations, and economic foundations, the main point is that Wuyuan used to belong to Huizhou, and many people from Huizhou do business abroad, especially from Wuyuan. Huizhou merchants in various ports have guild organizations and public funds, which are difficult to analyze. A sudden split would cause great losses and many disputes. Tens of thousands of Wuyuan overseas Chinese have no group protection and will inevitably be isolated, or even lose their jobs, causing great panic in the region. Moreover, the economic foundation of the Wuyuan people is built on commerce, which is the same as other counties in Huizhou, which is different from the counties in eastern Jiangxi, where the land is balanced and the soil is fertile, and the economic foundation of the people is built on agriculture. If they are combined, the lives of the Wuyuan people may be shaken. It is found that administrative divisions and the organizational structure of people's groups in various counties are two completely different things. Since the founding of the Republic of China, the old Huizhou Prefecture system has been abolished. More than 20 years have passed since then. The guilds and public funds in the six counties of Huizhou still exist, and there has been no analysis or disputes. This reassignment to Jiangxi Province is nothing more than a change in the administrative region of the province. The people of the six counties of Huizhou can still maintain their past organizations in fact, and the law does not force their separation. With the same economic foundation, the people of county A and county B can each engage in different occupations without affecting each other. Even within the same county, the people who engage in agriculture, industry, and commerce each have their own freedom of will and environment. A cannot force B to engage in the same occupation, let alone between counties. (C) Cultural Issues: The main point is that the cultural spirit of Anhui and the organizations of overseas Chinese groups all take Zhu Xi as their model. Wuyuan is the hometown of Zhu Xi, and the remnants of his style have not yet been extinguished. Huizhou's view of Wuyuan is like Donglu's view of Qufu and Southern Guangdong's view of Zhongshan. In recent years, it has been on the verge of bandit areas and has not been reduced to banditry, which is also due to this. Once reassigned, it will not only eliminate the cultural reputation of Anhui Province in history, but also shake the spiritual and material basis of the entire Anhui group at home and abroad. Moreover, the people in Leping, Dexing, and Fuliang in Jiangxi are mostly strong and brave in private fights, seeking revenge, and the law can hardly stop them. If Wuyuan is assigned to Jiangxi, I am afraid that it will not be able to withstand the deterioration. It is found that Zhu Xi is a famous Confucian scholar in our country, and his teachings have been spread widely and far. People in the country are proud of the sages, and no matter which province they belong to, they can admire and inherit them, and carry forward their legacy. There is no need to embrace feudal ideas and forcibly divide the boundaries, and occupy the sages for the private possession of an area. Our people's psychology of worshiping sages lies in admiring their great personality and good words and deeds. Goodness in the world is one. When Wuyuan belongs to Anhui, the people of Anhui can worship Zhu Xi, and they cannot prevent people from outside Anhui from worshiping Zhu Xi, and it will not add to the cultural reputation of Anhui Province. When Wuyuan belongs to Jiangxi, the people of Anhui can still worship Zhu Xi, and the people of Jiangxi cannot prevent the people of Anhui from worshiping Zhu Xi, and it will not damage the cultural reputation of Anhui Province. Anhui and Jiangxi both belong to the territory of China. Why should we have tribal views and fight over stories? As for the worry of being deteriorated after the reassignment, this is absolutely impossible. Whether Wuyuan's education is better than Dexing, Leping, and Fuliang is still to be investigated in fact. Assuming that it is better, then the knowledge of the people of Wuyuan must be higher than that of the neighboring counties. What deterioration can be worried about? (D) Historical Relationship: The main point is that political facilities must focus on historical relationships. Wuyuan was established from the Tang Dynasty to the Five Dynasties and belonged to She Prefecture. In the Song Dynasty, it belonged to Huizhou Xin'an Prefecture. In the Yuan Dynasty, it belonged to Huizhou Road. In the Ming Dynasty, it belonged to Huizhou Prefecture. Until the Qing Dynasty, Wuyuan always belonged to the Huizhou region and belonged to the jurisdiction of Anhui without any changes. The history is deep, and the administration is convenient day by day. A sudden change will cause many separations. It is found that political facilities should focus on historical relationships. However, measuring the situation, considering the gains and losses, to adapt to the needs of the facts is also a necessary action in administration. How can there be no changing laws in the world, and there is absolutely no permanent rule to stick to? Wuyuan's reassignment has its own factual needs. It cannot be based on historical evolution and ignore reality. Since the founding of the Republic of China, there have been many changes in provincial administrative regions. The largest ones are the establishment of provinces in Rehe, Chahar, Suiyuan, Ningxia, and Chuanbian, and the establishment of municipalities in Nanjing, Shanghai, Qingdao, and Beiping. If it is beneficial to the country, we should actively improve it and not allow ourselves to stick to the old and follow the routine and stick to the status quo. All four of these are the reasons for their inappropriateness, so I will give them detailed guidance, so that the people of the county can understand the purpose of this headquarters to reorganize the administrative divisions.

To sum up the two sections above, it is clear that Wuyuan's reassignment is indeed adapting to the needs, and the requesting documents are actually mostly empty and superficial. The true meaning is revealed by mutual elucidation. Moreover, the Executive Yuan has already replied to the record, which is even more firm and unwavering. Therefore, the county government is ordered to know and inform, and to extensively publicize the various sections in the order and provide detailed guidance, so that all know where the general meaning lies, and there must be no prejudice. Even in the future, when the two provinces cooperate fully, there will still be no boundaries between them. The chairman, Chiang Kai-shek, (23rd Datong News Agency)

He and Xu Return to Hankou from Xunyang 104

Visited Chiang in Lushan to Discuss Bandit Suppression Plans

He Will Go to Northern Hubei in a Few Days, Xu Returns to Western Hubei

Hankou Dispatch: The Pacification Director stationed in Hubei, He Chengjun, and the Commander-in-Chief of the Bandit Suppression in the Hubei-Hunan Border Area, Xu Yuanquan, previously went to Xunyang on the 10th to attend a bandit suppression conference to be convened by Chairman Chiang in Lushan. Zhang Xueliang, the Deputy Commander of Bandit Suppression in the three provinces, also went by plane on the 15th. He and Xu visited Chiang several times in Lushan to discuss the bandit suppression plans in western and northern Hubei. They went down the mountain together on the 22nd and took the Ruihe ship westward from Xunyang, arriving in Hankou at 1:00 p.m. on the 23rd. According to (1) He, this trip to Guling was to visit Chairman Chiang to report on the inspection of western and northern Hubei and to ask for instructions on future clean-up and rehabilitation measures. Chairman Chiang gave very detailed instructions and especially instructed to actively develop highways and facilitate transportation. The Jiangxi bandits have suffered heavy losses after repeated attacks and suppression. He Yunqiao has contacted the Guangdong and Guangxi sides to prepare to mobilize a pincer attack, which can be dispatched at any time. The long encirclement has been completed, and the bandit disaster can be eliminated. The bandit suppression military affairs in Sichuan Province have also been successful. The defenses on the border between Henan, Hubei, and Shaanxi are consolidated and will not allow them to disturb. After Xiao Zhichu's troops take over the defense of Yunyang, I will still go to northern Hubei for inspection. Deputy Commander Zhang and General Commander Liu Xueya met in Lushan. Zhang still needs to stay for a while to discuss with Chiang. Liu is suffering from a minor illness and is recuperating. Chiang attaches great importance to the floods and droughts in Hubei Province and is discussing relief measures. (2) Xu said that he visited Chiang to report on the clean-up of scattered bandits in northwestern Hubei and the prevention of the remnant bandits of Xu and He, and to present a report on the rehabilitation and the construction of highways, which was well received. The mountain roads in western Hubei are rugged and inconvenient for military transportation. In the past, remnant bandits harassed the area, which was probably the reason. Now that the scattered bandits have been cleared and Xu and He have fled far away, it is appropriate to develop transportation in time and strengthen the arrangements. The road line from Shinan to Badong is the most important. If this road is completed, it will be like increasing the bandit suppression force by several times. It is planned to consult with Chairman Zhang Yuejun in Hankou to proceed, and then return to Shashi for defense. The regimental and battalion commanders and chiefs of staff of the second term of the 41st and 48th divisions of the 10th Army, led by Zhang Zhenhan, commander of the 41st division, arrived in Hankou and will go to Xunyang for training in a few days. (23rd)

The War Zone Relief Committee Ends 105

750,000 in Labor Relief in Hebei and Chahar Have Not Yet Been Completed

The North China Agricultural Cooperation Committee is About to be Established

Beiping Dispatch: The War Zone Relief Committee held a closing meeting at the committee at 10:00 a.m. today (21st). Chairman Huang Fu telegraphed Vice Chairman Yu Xuezhong to preside on his behalf. Yu arrived in Ping yesterday evening from Tianjin and attended the meeting this morning. Members Zhang Boling, Song Zheyuan, Jiang Menglin, Zhang Yuanshan, Tao Menghe, Zhou Yichun, Shi Jinghuan, Zhou Zuomin, and Secretary General Xia Qingyi also attended the meeting. Chairman Yu Xuezhong's agenda: (1) Each group reported on the closing work, which will be completely closed from today. (2) The chairman reported that after the end of this committee, it was decided to organize the North China Agricultural Cooperation Enterprise Committee to promote cooperative enterprises for farmers in North China. All members of the committee are appointed. Those who have been appointed are Zhang Boling, Zhuang Menglin, Tao Menghe, Zhou Yichun, Shi Jinghuan, Qin Dechun, Xia Qingyi, Zhou Zuomin, and Zhang Yuanshan. It is planned that Zhang Boling will be the chairman. The founding meeting will be held at the Political Consolidation Council next Monday at 4:00 p.m. (3) The continued work of labor relief will be transferred to the Hebei Provincial Government. The meeting adjourned at 12:00 noon. After the meeting, telegrams were sent to the Executive Yuan and the Political Consolidation Council, and letters were sent to various agencies, reporting on the closing process. In addition, in the name of Vice Chairman Yu Xuezhong, the committee's establishment process and work situation were published. The original text is as follows: "This committee was established on July 21, 1933. At the same time, the Secretariat was established, focusing on the internal organization. On August 7, the Emergency Relief Group was established. On the 17th, the Finance Group was established. The Agricultural Relief Group began preparations on August 4 and was organized on September 1. This is the situation at the beginning of the operation. On August 17, 1 million yuan was allocated by the Ministry of Finance. On January 17, 1934, 2 million yuan was collected from the public debt mortgage. Donations from all parties continued to be received, totaling more than 140,000 yuan. This is the income situation. When the 1 million yuan allocated by the Ministry of Finance was received, it was decided to give priority to emergency relief. The emergency relief items were stipulated as three items: cash and food, health care, and labor relief. The investigation of the cash and food item began on August 31. A total of more than 430,000 yuan in cash and more than 30,000 yuan in food were distributed in 22 counties in Hebei, which have all been completed. The health care item began on September 14. A total of 86,700 people were diagnosed and vaccinated in 17 counties, including Luan County in Hebei Province, at a cost of 4,500 yuan, which has long been completed. Under the labor relief item, it was stipulated as three items: river management, road repair, repair of public buildings, and filling in trenches. A total of more than 770,000 yuan was allocated to Hebei and Chahar provinces, which have not yet been completed. At the beginning of the establishment of the Agricultural Relief Group, it was only able to allocate donations from all parties for investigation and preparation. It was not until the public debt mortgage was allocated to the committee that it could be implemented. A total of 3,793 mutual aid societies were established in 24 counties in Hebei and 9 counties in Chahar, with more than 179,000 guarantors and more than 1.419 million yuan in loans, which were all completed by June 15. This is the process. The working period of this committee was originally set for six months, and it could be extended if necessary. As of January 21 this year, the six-month period expired, but the public debt mortgage was just allocated, and the relief work was in progress. Therefore, it was submitted to the Executive Yuan and approved to extend it for two months, until March 21. When the extension expired, the agricultural relief was only extended to Luandong, and the agricultural relief in the counties north of the Great Wall in Chahar was added. When the affairs were busy, the labor relief had to wait for the spring thaw before it could start. It was submitted to the Executive Yuan again to extend it for two months, and when it expired on May 21, most of the emergency relief and agricultural relief had been completed, but there were still problems with a part of the labor relief plan. Moreover, the War Zone Relief Bonds had a face value of 4 million yuan, and the Ministry of Finance limited them to be sold at more than 80% off. At that time, they had not yet been sold. This committee was negotiating back and forth by telegram. If the money was obtained after the sale, the work of this committee would not be over. It was submitted to the Executive Yuan again to extend it for another two months. During these two months, it was decided to change a part of the labor relief plan to the Qinglong Bay, Qilihai, and South New Diversion River projects, which were handled by the Construction Department of the Hebei Provincial Government and the North China Water Conservancy Commission. This committee has already allocated the funds, and it is estimated that it will still take time to complete the project. The banks mortgaging the public debt required the Ministry of Finance to include it in the Public Debt Fund for guarantee before they could negotiate. This committee transferred the negotiation to the Ministry of Finance, but it was not approved. This committee also asked the Ministry of Finance to sell it in Shanghai, but it was not approved. Recently, it was approved by telegram, stating that if your committee has not sold it by the time it expires, it will not be allowed to be sold. This committee has no need to wait any longer. When this committee's closing method was telegraphed to the Executive Yuan, it was approved. It should be closed on time. In addition to compiling and printing this committee's general report, which contains detailed information, and distributing it for inspection, I would like to report on the general outline first." (21st)

Abolishing Oppressive Taxes in Fujian Province 106

First Batch of Twenty-Seven Items Abolished

Fuzhou Correspondence: The Fujian Provincial Department of Finance, in order to comply with the national financial conference's resolution to abolish oppressive taxes and reduce the people's suffering, has specially formulated a provincial tax survey form, ordering all county governments and tax bureaus to fill it out in detail in preparation for exemptions. Now, according to successive reports submitted by various counties, the Fujian Local Economic Research Association established by the department has discussed the matter and decided that the first batch to be abolished includes twenty-seven items: (1) Provincial Ship Tax, annual amount of 200,000 yuan; (2) Minhou Flower Seed Tax, annual amount of 480 yuan; (3) Minhou Chicken, Duck, and Goose Tax, annual amount of 4,000 yuan; (4) Minhou Bean Sprout Tax, annual amount of 48 yuan; (5) Minhou Retail Wine and Food Tax, annual amount of 600 yuan; (6) Minhou Retail Cigarette Tax, annual amount of 480 yuan; (7) Minhou Rickshaw Tax, annual amount of 1,200 yuan; (8) Minhou Vegetable Vendor Tax, annual amount of 360 yuan; (9) Minhou Magnolia Tax, annual amount of 480 yuan; (10) Minhou Paper Umbrella Tax, annual amount of 216 yuan; (11) Minhou Fermented Bean Curd Tax, annual amount of 204 yuan; (12) Minhou Meat Swallow (Wan) Tax, annual amount of 312 yuan; (13) Minhou Paint Tax, annual amount of 144 yuan; (14) Minhou Fresh Fruit Tax, annual amount of 360 yuan; (15) Minhou Ready-Made Clothing Tax, annual amount of 240 yuan; (16) Minhou Milk Tax, annual amount of 240 yuan; (17) Minhou

Potato Tax, annual amount of 360 yuan; (18) Minhou Rattan Ware Tax, annual amount of 120 yuan; (19) Minhou Hair Net Tax, annual amount of 33.6 yuan; (20) Minhou Knitting Tax, annual amount of 93 yuan; (21) Minhou Fake Straw Suitcase Tax, annual amount of 55 yuan; (22) Minhou Gong Tax, annual amount of 72 yuan; (23) Minhou Fake Snow Flake Tax, annual amount of 31.2 yuan; (24) Minhou Bamboo Mat Tax, annual amount of 84 yuan; (25) Minhou Copper Casting Tax, annual amount of 30 yuan; (26) Minhou Bamboo Strip Tax, annual amount of 81.6 yuan; (27) Minhou Brush and Ink Tax, annual amount of 146.4 yuan. The total annual amount of the above twenty-seven items is 210,469.8 yuan, which has been listed and reported to the Executive Yuan's Ministry of Finance for examination and compliance. However, of the above twenty-seven items, only the ship tax is provincial, while the remaining twenty-six items are business taxes collected by the Minhou County Tax Bureau. In addition, there are many other types of oppressive taxes in various counties that are being investigated. As for the land tax surcharge, which is most closely related to the rural economy, there are four types of general surcharges throughout the province: highway, education, autonomy, and group affairs. It is still difficult to ascertain those added separately by each county. The Department of Finance is currently discussing solutions with the relevant Departments of Civil Affairs, Education, and Construction. Furthermore, regarding deed taxes, taxes are often collected not through deed verification but by assigning quotas to villages and households. The stamp tax is also not strictly enforced through the purchase of stamps, but rather merchants are forced to recognize quotas on a monthly basis or according to gang distribution, causing great disturbance to farmers and merchants. Therefore, the public is also eager for the authorities to correct this. (July 14th)

Opium Trafficker Apprehended in a Songjiang Hotel 107

Our county is preparing to implement a smoking ban. Yesterday, an opium trafficker named Wang Xinfa was apprehended at No. 9, Xie Sheng Hotel, outside the west gate of the city. Thirty-four packages of opium, weighing a total of thirty-four taels, were confiscated. The Second District police station escorted him to the Public Security Bureau and then to the county government for investigation. According to his confession, Wang Xinfa arrived in Songjiang yesterday on foot from Shanghai and was staying for one night, planning to go to Hangzhou to sell it. He was caught midway and is currently detained.

Changshu Forcibly Registers Opium Smokers 108

The Changshu County Opium Prohibition Association has been in operation for over a month since its establishment. Currently, after a re-examination, there are over 17,000 opium smokers in the entire county. The registration of opium smokers is now underway. However, many opium smokers are taking a wait-and-see attitude. Previously, the seventh meeting resolved to implement compulsory registration of opium smokers starting on August 1st. As for the establishment of opium paste stores, it has been decided that 35 locations will be set up throughout the county. However, there are currently over a hundred applications submitted. The association has decided to stop accepting applications from the 23rd and will determine the locations by drawing lots from the applications that have already been submitted.

Wuxi Fields Continue to Receive Bountiful Rain 109

In the city, rainfall began on the 21st of this month, and the Fahrenheit temperature dropped to 86 degrees. The next day, there was still a cool drizzle. In two days, the rainfall totaled about eight fen. However, it was not widespread in the countryside. Yesterday (the 23rd), the weather was clear and cool. After 3 AM, thunder rumbled, and heavy rain fell until 5:30 AM, with an estimated rainfall of over two inches. In the countryside, Rongxiang, Youjiadan, Changan Bridge, Nanqiao, and Qianqiao received three inches of rain, Yuqi received five fen, Qianzhou and Beiqifang received over an inch, Dongting received three inches, and the river level rose by five inches. Huadafangzhuang, Yangting, Yanqiao, and other places received two inches of rain, Bashi Bridge received three inches, and Dangkou and Ganlu received three inches. Zhangjing Bridge received two inches, and Anzhen received three inches. The rain was widespread in both urban and rural areas. Fields that had already been planted were sufficiently watered. Fields that had not yet been planted still could not be planted, but the soil was moistened, making it easier to plant after irrigating the fields. However, there is a lack of water-lifting machinery. It is hoped that another two or three inches of rain will fall in the coming days to remedy the situation. Xueyan Bridge, at the border of Wuxi and Changshu, also received three inches of rain. It is thought that Changshu, Cheng, Wuxi, and Suzhou counties have also received rain.

Trial Opens in Seduction of Female Student Case 110

Xu Yiting, the owner of the Xintai Xiang Lace Shop in Shanghai, has a son named Xu Yibin, a student at Fudan University. Xu Yibin seduced a local female student named Chen Xueqin, initially promising to marry her and writing a letter of intent, but then abandoned her. Chen's father filed a lawsuit in Shanghai with the Special First Court, accusing Xu Yibin of undermining public morals. After Judge Liu Yugui summoned him, he deemed that the case was under the wrong jurisdiction and ruled to transfer it to the local court in our county for trial. Yesterday (the 24th) at 9:30 AM, Judge Liu Bingzhen of the local branch court summoned Chen Shengyang and his daughter Chen Xueqin to conduct a preliminary investigation. Because the case concerned morals, the court ordered that the hearing be closed to the public. However, it was heard that Chen Xueqin testified in court about the details of her seduction by Xu. As a result, the court ordered her to return home and await the summons of the defendant before further questioning.

Station Set Up at Miaogang Bridge to Pump Water 111

The location for the water station in our county has been changed to Miaogang Bridge outside the East Gate. The five water pumps required have already been shipped from Shanghai to Wuxi. The largest has 25 horsepower, and the next largest has 24 horsepower. The Department of Construction ordered the Suzhou Agricultural Implement Manufacturing Plant to send staff member Xie Hewu and more than twenty mechanics to Wuxi to install the machines yesterday morning (the 24th). Two machines were installed on the shore, and three were installed on boats. Meanwhile, the Bureau of Construction hired more than thirty dam construction workers to build an earthen dam. It is expected that water can be drawn today to save the farmland in the northeast. In addition, the county government of our county has been ordered to purchase seeds for drought-resistant crops and has decided to first purchase 300 dan of buckwheat seeds for distribution to various districts for planting. As for mung bean and adzuki bean seeds, the purchase will be temporarily postponed.

Changzhou Disaster Prevention Committee Purchases Miscellaneous Grain Seeds 112

The Wu Ba Disaster Prevention Committee held another meeting on the 23rd. At that time, it was noted that the number of affected fields in our county was very large, and miscellaneous grain seeds should be purchased and distributed to farmers for replanting. The committee decided to purchase 500 dan of buckwheat, 500 dan of mung beans, and 200 dan of potatoes to determine the quantity of seeds and how to distribute them. It was determined that He Zhaoxi, the director of the Agricultural Extension Institute, would be responsible for purchasing and distributing the seeds, which would be sold at the original price. Half of the cash would be collected in advance, with the district chief or other responsible agency guaranteeing the price. The remaining half would be the responsibility of the guarantor after the autumn harvest. The method for distributing the quantity of seeds will be handled by the inspectors of the committee and the director of the Agricultural Extension Institute, based on the actual disaster conditions in each district.

Drought in Jiangbei Counties of Nantong Relieved 113

The counties of Tong, Ru, Tai, Hai, Qi, and Jing in Jiangbei have suffered from severe drought and heat, creating an unprecedented drought situation. Fortunately, in the past week, there has been continuous rain, and the farmland has been sufficiently moistened. The cotton seedlings have recovered after the rain, and if there are no unexpected disasters in the future, there is still a 70% chance of a good harvest. In the coastal reclamation areas of Huainan, there has also been soaking rain, and the cotton crop situation has improved.

Lang Mountain About to Fall into the River 114

The collapse of the riverbank in Nantong is becoming more and more severe in recent days. Lang Mountain, towering on the riverbank, will soon fall into the river. People along the river have been requesting relief from the provincial and county governments and the Nantong District Commissioner's Office.

Electric Water Pump Used to Irrigate the River 115

Although the continuous rainfall in Tong County has sufficiently moistened the farmland, the rivers in the area are still drying up rapidly. Local communities have pooled funds to purchase pumps, which have been installed in Yao Port. Using electric power, they are pumping water from the Yangtze River into the inner rivers day and night to facilitate irrigation of farmland and commercial transportation. Within three days, all the large and small rivers in the county will be navigable.

Aviation Lottery Case Investigation Concluded 116

The Nantong branch of the Bank of China discovered that one of the Fifth Prize tickets of the Third Aviation Lottery, No. 227404, had been altered from No. 27104. The prosecutor has filed a public lawsuit against the ticket holder, Shi Mingqing, and the person collecting the prize money on his behalf, Yang Youheng, in the Criminal Court. On the 23rd, Judge Long questioned them. Yu Chongwei, the president of the Bank of China, also attended the court. The court declared the debate concluded and scheduled the verdict for the 28th.

Over Ten Zhang of Zhenjiang River Embankment Collapses Violently 117

In recent years, the riverbank around Jiaxing Bridge in Jiangbei has been collapsing annually, and this is especially severe this year. The other day, over ten zhang of the area collapsed violently again, making prevention impossible and leaving it in an unmanageable state. In addition, the riverbank in Hehua Pond in the county's seventh district is also being eroded by huge waves and swirling currents, resulting in frequent collapses.

Security Department Reorganizes Zhenjiang Merchant Corps 118

In order to strengthen the self-defense capabilities of merchants and residents, Xiang Zhizhuang, the director of the Jiangsu Security Department, is reorganizing the Zhenjiang Merchant Corps. He previously personally inspected the corps and deemed it necessary to provide training. It is reported that the training period was originally scheduled to begin on August 1st, but due to the summer vacation, the training could not be carried out as scheduled. It will likely be held after the Chamber of Commerce election. As for the training method, members of each corps will be drawn from various merchants based on the size and number of people in each business. Each business with five or more people will send one person for training, which will last for three months. After graduation, they will return to work in their respective businesses, and others will be selected for the second batch of training.

Yangzhou Wireless Radio Station Moves Back to the Canals and Works Bureau 119

The Jiangbei Canals and Works Bureau, in order to facilitate the rapid transmission of information during the tense summer flood season, has obtained approval from the provincial government to move the wireless radio station, which was relocated to Wu Zhuang by the Bureau, back to the Canals and Works Bureau. This is to facilitate the receipt and dispatch of information regarding water conditions and flood control projects. Yesterday (the 23rd), the station director, Shen Hongxiang, led the mechanics Zhang Jinqing and others to move all the station's equipment to Yangzhou and install it overnight in the Bureau. On the 23rd, the station resumed receiving and sending radio messages as usual.

Detailed Account of the Rice Riot in Wangdian, Jiaxing 120

On the 22nd, two to three hundred villagers arrived in Wangdian Town, Jiaxing, to demand rice from various rice shops, creating a serious situation. All the rice shops in the town immediately closed down. Later, after local people made great efforts to persuade them to leave, there were still a few poor villagers who did not disperse. After finding a way to give each person two sheng of rice, they finally left. The county government immediately dispatched representatives Mei Shouren and Lu Chujue to investigate on the 23rd. Unexpectedly, on the 23rd, over two thousand villagers from the Hai and Yan areas and the Yu Xian district arrived in the town (including salt traffickers and Hunan gangs). They broke into the rice shops of Pan Yaji (over one hundred shi of rice, over one hundred shi of beans, and over ten pieces of clothing were looted), Ding Heshun (over twenty shi of rice, over ten shi of beans, and over thirty silver dollars were looted), Yuan Tailong (over six shi of rice and over one shi of beans were looted), and Chen Yuantai (over one hundred shi of rice and over two hundred shi of beans were looted) in Dongli, Xili, Nantang, and Beitang, looting rice and beans. The shops throughout the town closed their doors one after another. The county's basic team and water police rushed from Jiaxing to the town. By noon, the villagers had dispersed. The police arrested six people, including Sun Ashun, Gao Asan, Shen Xilin, Yu Zuobin, Zhang Aliu, and Hu Asong, on the spot and sent them to the Public Security Bureau for detention. At the same time, the two representatives, Lu and Mei, convened a meeting of local people in the district office. As a result, it was decided to set up two porridge kitchens in the east and west to provide relief to poor farmers. The rice will be donated and supplied by the rice shops. The police and local guards will temporarily remain in the town to maintain order. On the other hand, the shops were encouraged to resume business as usual to maintain the market. The porridge kitchens are currently being actively prepared and will be established soon.

Conflict Between Villagers Seeking Rain and Tax Police in Haimen 121

Due to the prolonged drought, about five hundred villagers from near Dong'an Town in Qidong gathered at the local temple to pray for rain on the afternoon of the 18th. A detachment of tax police stationed in the temple prevented the villagers from entering, resulting in a conflict between the two sides. More and more villagers gathered, trying to rush into the temple. Seeing that the situation was not good, the tax police opened fire, wounding five people. The villagers became even more enraged and captured two tax police messengers, beating them until they were injured. The situation became more and more serious. When County Magistrate Li learned of the incident, he rushed to the scene of the incident with Zhu Chuliang, the chairman of the Chamber of Commerce, to persuade the villagers to hand over the messengers to the county government for processing. The injured villagers were sent to the county to verify their injuries and handle the matter fairly. The tax police were ordered not to take the above actions again. The villagers were satisfied and dispersed.

Taixing County Magistrate Cares About the People's Suffering 122

Since taking office, County Magistrate Wang Lanqing has strived to improve all aspects of administration. Recently, due to the prolonged lack of rain and drought, in addition to preventing epidemics from occurring, he personally went to the countryside to comfort the farmers.

Ningbo Bandits Rob and Kill Township Chief 123

On the afternoon of the 9th of this month, at around 11:00 PM, eight or nine bandits armed with guns, knives, and other weapons broke into the home of Shen Youren in Bansha Township, Daishan, the sixth district of Dinghai, and robbed it. They also stabbed Shen Youren and his mother, Mrs. Shen, and his wife, Mrs. Li. When the township chief, Shen Pinyuan, and his son, Shen Quanyou, heard the alarm, they planned to gather people to arrest the bandits. However, as soon as they reached the door, they were spotted by the bandits and shot dead. The Second Security Division has ordered a strict investigation and arrest of the perpetrators.

After Discovering His Wife's Adultery, He Killed Her and Then Himself 124

A woodworker named A'ao, the son of Wang Fusheng, a farmer from Shantou Yantou, Linshan, the fourth district of Yuyao, had a wife named Xuan, who was lewd by nature and had an affair with a local ruffian named Xie A'ru. In the afternoon of the 20th, Xie took advantage of A'ao and his father being out and came to meet with Xuan. Unexpectedly, just as they were enjoying their tryst, A'ao suddenly returned home and discovered their secret. Seeing that the situation was not good, Xie fled. A'ao was filled with shame and anger and was determined to kill her. He took an axe and struck his wife Xuan on the head, killing her instantly. Fearing punishment, he then used the axe to strike his own head violently. Blood flowed all over the ground, and both of them collapsed in pools of blood. By the time his father returned home, A'ao was barely breathing.

Hangzhou Xinyuan Gold Shop Detects Blackmail Suspect 125

Several years ago, the Xinyuan Gold Shop on Jianqiao Street was robbed of over ten thousand yuan in broad daylight. On the 21st of this month, the shop suddenly received a threatening letter signed "KG Group," demanding a loan of 300 silver dollars and stating that someone would come to collect it in person before 11:00 AM on the 23rd. The shop secretly reported this to the First Division of the Provincial Public Security Bureau, which dispatched a patrol officer and several plainclothes policemen to the shop. At the appointed time, a young man wearing a silk gown came to the shop and asked for the manager. He was immediately arrested by the police. He confessed his name was Liu Taoying, 25 years old, and that he had served in the military for many years. He had resorted to this because he could not find a job. He was transferred to the General Bureau for interrogation.

Cai Bingyan Inspects Hefei During the Heat of Summer 126

Fei and other places in Anhui have long been plagued by bandits. Every year, when the green crops grow tall, the bandits become rampant. Since Mr. Cai Bingyan took office as the Director of the Security Department, he has made great efforts to suppress and eliminate them, executing several bandit leaders. Now that the forests are dense again and the bandits are rampant, Mr. Cai is personally conducting inspections to provide guidance and ensure that the bandits are eradicated and the people can live and work in peace.

Father, Son, and Concubine Assassinated in Funing 127

In Daliang Village, Northwest Township, Yilin Town, there was a man named Liang Zengyao who had previously served as a battalion commander in the army of Ma Sanren, the garrison commander of Huaiyang. After returning home, he became the township chief of the village. Last night, more than ten thugs armed with guns broke into the Liang residence and, without saying a word, shot Liang Zengyao dead. They also killed his second son, Jin Chen, and his concubine, Mrs. Xu. The thugs headed north. It is heard that the family has come to the city to report to the county and request that the perpetrators be arrested and brought to justice.

Local News

Far East Aviation Company Demonstrates New Aircraft at Hongqiao Yesterday 128

Kong Xiangxi, Wu Tiecheng, and Others Attended the Viewing

The Program Included Stunt Flying, Which Was a Novelty

The British-owned Far East Aviation Company held a demonstration of its newly arrived Fawn Fox fighter aircraft at Hongqiao Airport yesterday at 5:30 PM. Finance Minister Kong Xiangxi, Mayor Wu Tiecheng, and hundreds of Chinese and foreign guests attended. The demonstration ended at around 6:00 PM due to rain, leaving the audience unsatisfied. Details are as follows:

Attending Guests 129

The company originally scheduled the demonstration for last Saturday, but it was changed to yesterday due to bad weather. Attendees yesterday included Finance Minister Kong Xiangxi, Mayor Wu Tiecheng, Secretary-General of the City Government Yu Hongjun, Director of the Aviation Department Zhang Huichang, Director of the Naval Aircraft Manufacturing Department Zeng Yijing, Director of the Public Security Bureau Wen Hongen, Section Chief of the City Government Li Dachao, British Consul-General Belinan, and hundreds of newspaper reporters, who were warmly received by Chinese Manager Zhou Guansan and others.

Airport Security 130

Yesterday afternoon, the Sixth District Police Station of the Municipal Public Security Bureau dispatched a large number of police officers to the airport and along Hongqiao Road to direct traffic. In addition, the Municipal Security Department and the Military Police Regiment also sent troops to the airport to provide security. Security was extremely tight. The Municipal Government Orchestra also attended to play music and enhance the excitement.

Hamilton Performs Stunt Flying (Photo by Ye Changlie) 131

Wonderful Performance 132

The company had previously erected a temporary mat shed on the south side of the airport as a place for guests to rest. Tea and snacks were set up on both sides of the shed. At 5:30 PM, the demonstration officially began. First, Sir Hamilton, an instructor at the Far East Aviation School in Hong Kong, piloted a new Avro trainer aircraft. The aircraft slowly rose from the airport and circled the airport sky once. Then, he performed various flying stunts, soaring to thousands of feet and then flying low over the heads of the audience. Each maneuver, whether flying upside down or sideways, was performed with ease. The dangerous maneuvers were met with applause and cheers. Then, he performed stunt flying, which was a novelty in Shanghai, flying only ten feet above the ground. The aircraft swayed its wings left and right like a drunk person walking at night, which was truly remarkable. After landing, Captain Peng Naide, the manager of the company, took off in a Fawn Fox fighter aircraft and performed a straight up and down maneuver at extremely high speed. Five minutes later, he performed various maneuvers of attacking enemy aircraft in combat. At around 6:00 PM, it suddenly started to rain, and the guests left the venue one after another. However, the two men continued to fly their planes, performing a chase and attack simulation. Finally, due to the heavy rain, they landed at 6:15 PM, leaving the audience unsatisfied.

Peng Naide Boarding the Airplane (Photo by Qi Chang)

Far East Company Receives Chinese and Foreign Guests (Photo by Xu Tianzhang) 133

Flying to Jiangxi Tomorrow 134

True Cholera Discovered at Hongkou Epidemic Hospital 135

Patient Zhang Xicai from Chongming Confirmed by Shanghai Municipal Council Laboratory

According to the Guo Wen News Agency, since the beginning of summer this year, the weather has been unusually hot due to drought. Coolies and others, due to poor food and lodging, often sleep on the sidewalks of the roads, exposed to turbid air and heat. As a result, many people have contracted various summer diseases. Although there are many epidemic prevention facilities in Shanghai, they are still overwhelmed. The Hongkou Epidemic Hospital in the eastern district of Shanghai has become a leader in this regard due to its location. According to its daily reports, the number of people seeking treatment, the quality of its facilities, the widespread trust it enjoys, and the excellent results it achieves are all remarkable. Therefore, those who investigate the epidemic situation in Shanghai often use the hospital as a standard. Recently, the wind and rain have been intermittent, and the weather has suddenly turned cooler. Outpatient visits to various hospitals have been less frequent. However, there have been some unusual cases of true cholera discovered in Hongkou. Dysentery and gastroenteritis have not decreased slightly. If the weather becomes hot and humid, the outbreak of epidemics will be unstoppable. Furthermore, there have been cases of death due to peritonitis caused by scraping, indicating that the outdated treatments are not being eliminated, which is a hidden worry for society.

It is reported that the patient with true cholera is named Zhang Xicai, a native of Chongming who works at the China Iron Works. He was admitted to the Hongkou Hospital for treatment on the 18th of this month and was discharged on the 22nd after recovering. The Shanghai Municipal Council's laboratory confirmed that his stool contained true cholera bacteria. The Shanghai Municipal Council's laboratory report was issued on the 23rd.

Rainfall in this Port Still Insufficient 136

The Weather Turned Hot Again Yesterday

According to the Guo Wen News Agency, due to the overcast weather and intermittent rain in the past three or four days, the heatwave has been swept away, and the maximum temperature has dropped below 90 degrees. Yesterday, the weather turned hot again, and the maximum temperature in the afternoon reached 91.6 degrees. Since the drought began last month, the total rainfall has only been 1.42 inches. The total rainfall from January 1st to the day before yesterday this year was 17.2 inches, while the average rainfall during the same period in the past 61 years was 27.3 inches. The difference is still significant, and the lack of rainfall is obvious.

Current Situation of Rong Zongjing's Shenxin and Other Factories After His Reinstatement 138

Factories Operate as Usual and the Financial Industry is Determined to Maintain Support

According to the New Sound News Agency, Rong Zongjing's 21 Shenxin Textile Mills and Fuxin and Maoxin Flour Mills were previously reported to have suffered heavy losses due to the economic panic. Mr. Rong even retired once, and there were widespread rumors that the government would intervene to provide relief and reorganization. In order to learn the details, the New Sound News Agency reporter inquired with relevant parties yesterday and recorded the responses from the financial industry and Rong Zongjing as follows:

Financial Circle Opinions 139

According to the opinions of leaders in the banking and money exchange industries, regardless of the government's attitude and policies towards the various Shen Xin factories, the financial sector must do its utmost to maintain their existence. The scale of the Shen Xin factories is large, employing a large number of workers, and purchasing vast quantities of raw materials and other goods annually. Directly and indirectly, millions of people rely on them for their livelihoods. Furthermore, a significant number of Shanghai's financial institutions have business dealings with Shen Xin. For example, the Bank of China and other banks have extended the most industrial loans to Shen Xin. If there were to be any instability, the banking and money exchange industries would be affected, and social stability and the entire commercial market would suffer. Moreover, Rong Zongjing is one of the few remaining industrialists of his stature in China today. In terms of the number of spinning spindles, he accounts for one-fifth of the national total. For the sake of national enterprises, both the government and the public must unanimously assist in their progress. Therefore, the banking industry's sincerity in supporting these factories will not change, regardless of future circumstances. As for the panic in the industrial sector, it is currently a global phenomenon. China experienced something similar more than a decade ago. During the European War, textile factories in China sprang up like mushrooms after rain, and the Shen Xin yarn factories also expanded significantly at that time. Foreign exchange rates were very low at the time, and the cost of raw materials and machinery was relatively low. When the European War ended, foreign exchange rates suddenly soared, and unpaid debts more than doubled, causing temporary financial difficulties. At that time, the banking industry did its best to maintain stability, and there were no adverse effects. Subsequently, market conditions improved, and the Shen Xin factories became more prosperous, expanding year by year, from four factories to nine today.

Rong Zongjing's Talk 140

Yesterday, Rong Zongjing told reporters, "I have been managing Shen Xin and other factories for over thirty years, and I have experienced many hardships. I have strived to develop the national economy and overcome foreign resistance. Although outsiders may not fully understand the details of this process, the general public should be aware of the struggles involved. In recent years, the textile industry has been in a difficult situation. Those engaged in the industry should do their best to fight for survival. In addition, the nation should also share the responsibility of maintaining this foundational industry, so that it can move forward with determination. This time, I am taking a temporary break due to a minor illness, and Mr. Wang Yuqing is taking over the management of the business. However, rumors have spread that Shen Xin's factories are not performing well and urgently need reorganization. This is truly laughable. The work and operations of each factory are still the same as before, and income and expenses are quite balanced. I don't know where these rumors come from. As for the staff and workers directly employed by the factories, there are no less than hundreds of thousands. According to the statistics for the twenty-first year, the raw materials used by the factories include 51.46 million yuan for cotton and 52 million yuan for wheat. In terms of national tax contributions, the import tax on foreign cotton is 3 million yuan per year, the factory tax on yarn, cloth, and flour is over 5.56 million yuan per year, and the import tax on machinery is over 3.5 million yuan, totaling over 13 million yuan. Over the decades of operation, there has been some benefit to the national economy and the people's livelihood."

Poor Cotton Harvest in Jiangsu and Zhejiang 141

Tall Stalks and Lush Leaves in Shanxi and Shaanxi

According to the Central News Agency, the National Economic Commission's Cotton Control Committee reports that in order to improve the cotton industry nationwide, the committee purchased high-quality cotton seeds this spring and distributed them to Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Shanxi, Shaanxi, Hubei, and Henan provinces for planting. According to investigations, due to a month-long drought this summer, the cotton stalks in Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces could not grow tall, and the harvest is expected to be poor. However, in Shanxi, Shaanxi, and Henan provinces, the stalks are tall and the leaves are lush, with flourishing growth, and a bountiful harvest is expected.

Gu Xinyi Expresses His Opinion on Ordering Foreign Rice 142

Says He Has Never Had Preconceived Notions

According to the Central News Agency, yesterday, Gu Xinyi, chairman of the Bean and Rice Industry Association, made the following statement regarding the ordering of foreign rice. Gu said, "I have never had preconceived notions about ordering foreign rice. However, the bankruptcy of the rural economy is an undeniable fact. During this lean season, most poor farmers have long run out of grain and are borrowing rice to survive. Although there is rice in storage in various places, it is only in the hands of wealthy hoarders. Now, with the sudden drought, rice prices have soared, making life even more difficult for the poor farmers. The only beneficiaries are a very small number of hoarders. The association has been ordered to control rice prices and has decided on both short-term and long-term measures. The long-term measure is to order foreign rice to suppress rice prices, which is to help the rural economy. This is entirely consistent with the government's intention to revitalize the rural economy. The association previously requested an increase in import duties on foreign rice, and now it is requesting the ordering of foreign rice, only because the times are different, but the fundamental principle of helping the rural economy remains the same. Now, I see reports that the rice industry in this city held a meeting at Ren Gu Tang to discuss the case of opposing the ordering of foreign rice to prevent famine, and decided to postpone the ordering to maintain the livelihoods of farmers. However, the people who attended the meeting at Ren Gu Tang were the same people who unanimously supported the ordering of foreign rice at the association's special meeting the other day. Why is there such a change? I have not yet understood the reason. As for the opposition expressed by rice merchants in various counties, they mostly claim that there is still a lot of rice in storage in various places. They don't realize that all the stored rice is in the hands of hoarders. How can they guarantee that they will not hoard and monopolize, harming the poor farmers? I am afraid that the only beneficiaries will be the hoarders, and the so-called saving the livelihoods of farmers will be empty words. If those who oppose it can guarantee a balanced rice price and prevent grain prices from harming the people, then I will never have any preconceived notions about ordering foreign rice."

Yang Yihui Talks About the Recent Situation in Japan 144

The Japanese Government and Public Are Fanatically Preparing for War, Targeting Russia and the United States, with China Being Merely a Prize

According to Shen Shi News Agency, Yang Yihui, a cadre of the Youth Association, was sent to Japan some time ago to conduct an inspection. He was seriously injured in Japan after being hit by a car, but has now recovered. He returned to China yesterday. A reporter from Shen Shi News Agency went to interview him. Mr. Yang described in detail the fanatic state of war preparation among the Japanese government and public, as well as the economic panic within the country. The details are recorded as follows:

Japanese War Preparations 145

According to Mr. Yang, the Japanese government and public are united in their fanatic war preparation for the Second World War in 1960, which has reached an extreme level. Recently, war slogans with a strong sense of mobilization have been posted everywhere in the streets of cities across the country. In addition, almost all radio broadcasting stations have been controlled by the government, specializing in broadcasting war knowledge and air defense preparations, as well as various warning lectures on the seriousness of Japan's position in this war. Moreover, in various public amusement parks, there are special war experiment shows, which are very common. Children are welcome to enter for free, and military personnel conduct exercises on poison gas and machine guns, so that ordinary children develop a war mentality. All Japanese media are also largely controlled by the government, actively creating and promoting war-mongering opinions. Even entertainment venues such as movie theaters are used as tools to promote war preparation. For example, the famous film "The Last Command" recently shown in Japan tells the story of a group of children fighting for a bottle of milk, with the explanation that Japanese people will starve to death if they do not go to war. The film also depicts various non-factual renderings of Chinese people killing Japanese people, raping Japanese women, and abusing Japanese children, doing everything possible to provoke. Currently, the Japanese government and public have reached a unanimous attitude in their fanatic war preparation, and have scheduled three days of public war preparation exercises starting on July 26. The dissemination of this war ideology is centered on teaching shrines and Buddhist societies as its activity centers. The targets of its war preparation are no more than Russia and the United States. China is merely a prize in its pocket.

Overproduction 146

Regarding the economy, due to the extreme development of the machine industry, all Japanese factories and businesses have formed a very serious state of overproduction. Currently, industrial products are piling up in major commercial ports such as Tokyo, Osaka, and Nagasaki, and are urgently awaiting large-scale shipment and dumping abroad. However, due to the widespread resistance of various countries to Japanese goods, Japanese merchants are in a rather difficult situation. Therefore, they have recently developed another plan to entice wealthy merchants in the South Pacific islands to invest in Japanese factories, so that they can use the South Pacific islands as a dumping ground for their excess goods. Therefore, the sales of our country's domestic products in the South Pacific will be greatly affected. According to Mr. Yang, during the week before he left Japan, the Japanese took advantage of our country's revision of the new tariff and shipped a large number of Japanese goods and daily necessities to China for promotion and sales. Under the active and intensified dumping of Japanese goods, the future of our country's domestic products is very worrying.

Recovery and Return 147

This time, Mr. Yang was sent by the General Association of the Chinese Christian Youth Association to Japan to investigate the political and economic situation. In Tokyo, he was seriously injured on the street by a Japanese car driver, suffering severe injuries to his arm and chest. At that time, his injuries were very dangerous. After being hospitalized for three weeks and receiving surgical treatment, he escaped danger. At that time, many Japanese people expressed their condolences to Mr. Yang. As for the medical expenses incurred, because the driver who caused the accident was in a very difficult situation, Mr. Yang himself bore all the expenses. Recently, his chest injuries have healed, so he immediately set off to return home. After a few days of recuperation, his arm is also expected to recover.

The Zhapu Road Disturbance Case: Pelham is Suspended 150

How Do Chinese Citizens Feel About This Punishment of a Western Detective?

According to the "Great American Evening Post," Pelham, the Western detective who attempted to arrest two Japanese sailors who assaulted a Chinese woman on Zhapu Road in Hongkou about a month ago, has now been suspended. This morning (24th), a reporter from the "Great American Evening Post" inquired with Police Chief Gerrard and other senior police officers about the matter, but they were all silent. However, Sterling Fessenden, Director-General of the Shanghai Municipal Council, was still responsive. According to what he told the reporter from the "Great American Evening Post," the report of the committee investigating the Hongkou case may be discussed at the Shanghai Municipal Council meeting tomorrow. It is still difficult to predict whether a decision will be made to release any information to the press. According to police regulations, any police officer accused of dereliction of duty must automatically suspend himself while the case is being investigated. Mr. Fessenden's words imply that Detective Pelham has been suspended due to the police department's investigation of the Hongkou disturbance case. When asked whether Mr. Pelham's suspension was permanent, Mr. Fessenden replied that it would have to be determined later. It is reported that the current action is for ninety days. However, according to reliable sources, the investigation committee has determined that Mr. Pelham's attempt to arrest the Japanese sailors was illegal. The reasons are: (1) Mr. Pelham attempted to arrest the perpetrators of a conflict that he did not witness; (2) Mr. Pelham did not take the Japanese sailors to the Japanese Naval Landing Force branch office on Zhapu Road, but attempted to send them to the Hongkou police station.

After the impeachment was filed by the Control Yuan, the banking syndicate considered the guarantee to remain valid. The details are as follows:

Syndicate Guarantee 165

In July of last year, Railway Minister Gu Mengyu borrowed 50 million francs, or 10 million yuan in national currency, from the Paris Industrial Electrical Factory for the construction of the Datong-Tongguan section of the railway, with the income of the Zhengtai Railway as collateral, and a banking syndicate was organized by five banks, including the Bank of China, the Bank of Communications, the Bank of China and South Asia, the Jincheng Bank, and the Salt Industry Bank, to guarantee the payment and sign a guarantee contract. The Bank of Communications was the representative of the banking syndicate.

After Impeachment 166

If there were any malpractices, the banking syndicate would never provide a guarantee. Although Minister Gu has been impeached, the banking syndicate's guarantee will continue to be valid.
